and returns a committed log entry\n    84→// channel and error channel. Proposals for log updates are sent over the\n    85→// provided the proposal channel. All log entries are replayed over the\n    86→// commit channel, followed by a nil message (to indicate the channel is\n    87→// current), then new log entries. To shutdown, close proposeC and read errorC.\n    88→func newRaftNode(id int, peers []string, join bool, getSnapshot func() ([]byte, error), proposeC <-chan string,\n    89→\tconfChangeC <-chan raftpb.ConfChange,\n    90→) (<-chan *commit, <-chan error, <-chan *snap.Snapshotter) {\n    91→\tcommitC := make(chan *commit)\n    92→\terrorC := make(chan error)\n    93→\n    94→\trc := &raftNode{\n    95→\t\tproposeC:    proposeC,\n    96→\t\tconfChangeC: confChangeC,\n    97→\t\tcommitC:     commitC,\n    98→\t\terrorC:      errorC,\n    99→\t\tid:          id,\n   100→\t\tpeers:       peers,\n   101→\t\tjoin:        join,\n   102→\t\twaldir:      fmt.Sprintf(\"raftexample-%d\", id),\n   103→\t\tsnapdir:     fmt.Sprintf(\"raftexample-%d-snap\", id),\n   104→\t\tgetSnapshot: getSnapshot,\n   105→\t\tsnapCount:   defaultSnapshotCount,\n   106→\t\tstopc:       make(chan struct{}),\n   107→\t\thttpstopc:   make(chan struct{}),\n   108→\t\thttpdonec:   make(chan struct{}),\n   109→\n   110→\t\tlogger: zap.NewExample(),\n   111→\n   112→\t\tsnapshotterReady: make(chan *snap.Snapshotter, 1),\n   113→\t\t// rest of structure populated after WAL replay\n   114→\t}\n   115→\tgo rc.startRaft()\n   116→\treturn commitC, errorC, rc.snapshotterReady\n   117→}\n   118→\n   119→func (rc *raftNode) saveSnap(snap raftpb.Snapshot) error {\n   120→\twalSnap := walpb.Snapshot{\n   121→\t\tIndex:     snap.Metadata.Index,\n   122→\t\tTerm:      snap.Metadata.Term,\n   123→\t\tConfState: &snap.Metadata.ConfState,\n   124→\t}\n   125→\t// save the snapshot file before writing the snapshot to the wal.\n   126→\t// This makes it possible for the snapshot file to become orphaned, but prevents\n   127→\t// a WAL snapshot entry from having no corresponding snapshot file.\n   128→\tif err := rc.snapshotter.SaveSnap(snap); Shutting down.\")\n   180→\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, false\n   181→\t\t\t\t}\n   182→\t\t\t\trc.transport.RemovePeer(types.ID(cc.NodeID))\n   183→\t\t\t}\n   184→\t\t}\n   185→\t}\n   186→\n   187→\tvar replays WAL entries into the raft instance.\n   247→func (rc *raftNode) replayWAL() *wal.WAL {\n   248→\tlog.Printf(\"replaying WAL of member %d\", rc.id)\n   249→\tsnapshot := rc.loadSnapshot()\n   250→\tw := rc.openWAL(snapshot)\n   251→\t_, st, ents, err := w.ReadAll()\n   252→\tif err != nil {\n   253→\t\tlog.Fatalf(\"raftexample: failed to read WAL (%v)\", err)\n   254→\t}\n   255→\trc.raftStorage = raft.NewMemoryStorage()\n   256→\tif snapshot != nil {\n   257→\t\trc.raftStorage.ApplySnapshot(*snapshot)\n   258→\t}\n   259→\trc.raftStorage.SetHardState(st)\n   260→\n   261→\t// append to storage so raft starts at the right place in log\n   262→\trc.raftStorage.Append(ents)\n   263→\n   264→\treturn w\n   265→}\n   266→\n   267→func (rc *raftNode) writeError(err error) {\n   268→\trc.stopHTTP()\n   269→\tclose(rc.commitC)\n   270→\trc.errorC <- err\n   271→\tclose(rc.errorC)\n   272→\trc.node.Stop()\n   273→}\n   274→\n   275→func (rc *raftNode) startRaft() {\n   276→\tif !fileutil.Exist(rc.snapdir) {\n   277→\t\tif err := os.Mkdir(rc.snapdir, 0o750); err != nil {\n   278→\t\t\tlog.Fatalf(\"raftexample: cannot create dir for snapshot (%v)\", err)\n   279→\t\t}\n   280→\t}\n   281→\trc.snapshotter = snap.New(zap.NewExample(), rc.snapdir)\n   282→\n   283→\toldwal := wal.Exist(rc.waldir)\n   284→\trc.wal = rc.replayWAL()\n   285→\n   286→\t// signal replay has finished\n   287→\trc.snapshotterReady <- rc.snapshotter\n   288→\n   289→\trpeers := make([]raft.Peer, len(rc.peers))\n   290→\tfor i := range rpeers {\n   291→\t\trpeers[i] = raft.Peer{ID: uint64(i + 1)}\n   292→\t}\n   293→\tc := &raft.Config{\n   294→\t\tID:                        uint64(rc.id),\n   295→\t\tElectionTick:              10,\n   296→\t\tHeartbeatTick:             1,\n   297→\t\tStorage:                   rc.raftStorage,\n   298→\t\tMaxSizePerMsg:             1024 * 1024,\n   299→\t\tMaxInflightMsgs:           256,\n   300→\t\tMaxUncommittedEntriesSize: 1 << 30,\n   301→\t}\n   302→\n   303→\tif oldwal || rc.join {\n   304→\t\trc.node = raft.RestartNode(c)\n   305→\t} else {\n   306→\t\trc.node = raft.StartNode(c, rpeers)\n   307→\t}\n   308→\n   309→\trc.transport = &rafthttp.Transport{\n   310→\t\tLogger:      rc.logger,\n   311→\t\tID:          types.ID(rc.id),\n   312→\t\tClusterID:   0x1000,\n   313→\t\tRaft:        rc,\n   314→\t\tServerStats: stats.NewServerStats(\"\", \"\"),\n   315→\t\tLeaderStats: stats.NewLeaderStats(zap.NewExample(), strconv.Itoa(rc.id)),\n   316→\t\tErrorC:      make(chan error),\n   317→\t}\n   318→\n   319→\trc.transport.Start()\n   320→\tfor i := range rc.peers {\n   321→\t\tif i+1 != rc.id {\n   322→\t\t\trc.transport.AddPeer(types.ID(i+1), []string{rc.peers[i]})\n   323→\t\t}\n   324→\t}\n   325→\n   326→\tgo rc.serveRaft()\n   327→\tgo rc.serveChannels()\n   328→}\n   329→\n   330→// stop closes http, closes all channels, and stops raft.\n   331→func (rc *raftNode) stop() {\n   332→\trc.stopHTTP()\n   333→\tclose(rc.commitC)\n   334→\tclose(rc.errorC)\n   335→\trc.node.Stop()\n   336→}\n   337→\n   338→func (rc *raftNode) stopHTTP() {\n   339→\trc.transport.Stop()\n   340→\tclose(rc.httpstopc)\n   341→\t<-rc.httpdonec\n   342→}\n   343→\n   344→func (rc *raftNode) publishSnapshot(snapshotToSave raftpb.Snapshot) {\n   345→\tif raft.IsEmptySnap(snapshotToSave) {\n   346→\t\treturn\n   347→\t}\n   348→\n   349→\tlog.Printf(\"publishing snapshot at index %d\", rc.snapshotIndex)\n   350→\tdefer log.Printf(\"finished publishing snapshot at index %d\", rc.snapshotIndex)\n   351→\n   352→\tif snapshotToSave.Metadata.Index <= rc.appliedIndex {\n   353→\t\tlog.Fatalf(\"snapshot index [%d] should > progress.appliedIndex [%d]\", snapshotToSave.Metadata.Index, rc.appliedIndex)\n   354→\t}\n   355→\trc.commitC <- nil // trigger kvstore to load snapshot\n   356→\n   357→\trc.confState = snapshotToSave.Metadata.ConfState\n   358→\trc.snapshotIndex = snapshotToSave.Metadata.Index\n   359→\trc.appliedIndex = snapshotToSave.Metadata.Index\n   360→}\n   361→\n   362→var snapshotCatchUpEntriesN uint64 = 10000\n   363→\n   364→func (rc *raftNode) maybeTriggerSnapshot(applyDoneC <-chan struct{}) {\n   365→\tif rc.appliedIndex-rc.snapshotIndex <= rc.snapCount {\n   366→\t\treturn\n   367→\t}\n   368→\n   369→\t// wait until all committed entries are applied (or server is closed)\n   370→\tif applyDoneC != nil {\n   371→\t\tselect {\n   372→\t\tcase <-applyDoneC:\n   373→\t\tcase <-rc.stopc:\n   374→\t\t\treturn\n   375→\t\t}\n   376→\t}\n   377→\n   378→\tlog.Printf(\"start snapshot [applied index: %d | last snapshot index: %d]\", rc.appliedIndex, rc.snapshotIndex)\n   379→\tdata, err := rc.getSnapshot()\n   380→\tif err != nil {\n   381→\t\tlog.Panic(err)\n   382→\t}\n   383→\tsnap, err := rc.raftStorage.CreateSnapshot(rc.appliedIndex, &rc.confState, data)\n   384→\tif err != nil {\n   385→\t\tpanic(err)\n   386→\t}\n   387→\tif err := rc.saveSnap(snap); err != nil {\n   388→\t\tpanic(err)\n   389→\t}\n   390→\n   391→\tcompactIndex := uint64(1)\n   392→\tif rc.appliedIndex > snapshotCatchUpEntriesN {\n   393→\t\tcompactIndex = rc.appliedIndex - snapshotCatchUpEntriesN\n   394→\t}\n   395→\tif err := rc.raftStorage.Compact(compactIndex); err != nil {\n   396→\t\tif !errors.Is(err, raft.ErrCompacted) {\n   397→\t\t\tpanic(err)\n   398→\t\t}\n   399→\t} else {\n   400→\t\tlog.Printf(\"compacted log at index %d\", compactIndex)\n   401→\t}\n   402→\n   403→\trc.snapshotIndex = rc.appliedIndex\n   404→}\n   405→\n   406→func (rc *raftNode) serveChannels() {\n   407→\tsnap, err := rc.raftStorage.Snapshot()\n   408→\tif err != nil {\n   409→\t\tpanic(err)\n   410→\t}\n   411→\trc.confState = snap.Metadata.ConfState\n   412→\trc.snapshotIndex = snap.Metadata.Index\n   413→\trc.appliedIndex = snap.Metadata.Index\n   414→\n   415→\tdefer rc.wal.Close()\n   416→\n   417→\tticker := time.NewTicker(100 * time.Millisecond)\n   418→\tdefer ticker.Stop()\n   419→\n   420→\t// send proposals over raft\n   421→\tgo func() {\n
